</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Walgreens Boots Alliance Fiscal 2021 First Quarter Results Exceed Expectations </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Company Accelerates Healthcare and Omnichannel Investments </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>First quarter results, year-over-year </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Sales increased 5.7&nbsp;percent to $36.3&nbsp;billion, up 5.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Loss per share was $0.36, compared to EPS of $0.95 in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT>
quarter, including a $1.73 per share charge from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen; Adjusted EPS decreased 11.2&nbsp;percent to $1.22, down 11.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting an estimated adverse <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of $0.26 to $0.30 per share </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Net cash provided by operating activities was $1.2&nbsp;billion, an increase of $134&nbsp;million; Free cash flow
was $763&nbsp;million, an increase of $90&nbsp;million, or 13&nbsp;percent </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Fiscal 2021 outlook </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company maintained guidance of low single-digit growth in adjusted earnings per share at constant currency rates.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Strategic transactions </I></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company executes portfolio transformation with divestiture of pharmaceutical wholesale business. For more
information click <U>here</U>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Company accelerates its investment in VillageMD and boosts the large-scale rollout of full-service primary care
clinics in stores. For more information click <U>here</U>. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">DEERFIELD, Ill., Jan. 7, 2021 - Walgreens Boots Alliance, Inc. (Nasdaq: WBA)
today announced financial results for the first quarter of fiscal 2021, which ended Nov. 30, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Executive Vice Chairman and CEO Stefano Pessina said,
&#147;Our first quarter results exceeded expectations as we continue to deliver on our strategic priorities. As announced yesterday we have taken a major step forward in our transformation; we are divesting our pharmaceutical wholesale business with
plans to use the proceeds to accelerate our investments in healthcare. While the business environment remains challenging, we are rising to the occasion with agility and discipline and we are confident in our outlook for adjusted EPS for the fiscal
year. Our role in the healthcare system has never been more important, as the communities we serve continue to turn to our trusted brands and expert pharmacists. I am so proud of our teams and the historic and critical role they are playing to help
the world emerge from the pandemic, administering <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> vaccinations to frontline healthcare workers and vulnerable members of our society.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Overview of First Quarter Results </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA had fiscal 2021
first quarter sales of $36.3&nbsp;billion, an increase of 5.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, and an increase of 5.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>, reflecting growth in Retail Pharmacy USA and Pharmaceutical Wholesale. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company had an operating
loss of $440&nbsp;million in the first quarter, compared to operating income of $1.0&nbsp;billion in the same quarter a year ago, entirely due to a $1.5&nbsp;billion charge from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen. Adjusted
operating income was $1.3&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 9.9&nbsp;percent from the same quarter a year ago and a decrease of 10.1&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net loss attributable to WBA<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP> was $308&nbsp;million for the first quarter of fiscal 2021 compared with
net profit of $845&nbsp;million in the same quarter a year ago. The loss was entirely due to the AmerisourceBergen charge. Loss per share was $0.36, compared to earnings per share (EPS) of $0.95 in the same quarter a year ago. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted net earnings decreased 13.9&nbsp;percent to $1.1&nbsp;billion, down 14.3&nbsp;percent on a constant
currency basis, compared with the same quarter a year ago. Adjusted EPS was $1.22, a decrease of 11.2&nbsp;percent on a reported basis and a decrease of 11.6&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, compared with the same quarter a year ago,
reflecting an estimated adverse <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact of $0.26 to $0.30 per share. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating
activities was $1.2&nbsp;billion in the first quarter and free cash flow was $763&nbsp;million, an increase of 13&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Company Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company maintained fiscal 2021
guidance of low single-digit growth in adjusted earnings per share at </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">constant currency rates, with the profile skewed to opportunity: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">The first quarter exceeded expectations, reflecting strength in Boots UK and Boots Opticians.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> (including the weaker cough, cold and flu season), the company anticipates first-half fiscal 2021 adjusted EPS to be broadly in line with prior expectations. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related lock-downs and restrictions, and by increased growth investments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Progress on
Strategic Priorities </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Selected highlights of the company&#146;s recent progress on strategic initiatives - creating neighborhood health destinations
around a more modern pharmacy, accelerating digitalization, transforming and restructuring the company&#146;s retail offering and transformational cost management - include the following: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Since <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> testing began, Walgreens has administered more than
2.8&nbsp;million tests. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

long-term care facilities in 49 states. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Walgreens launched myWalgreens, a complete reinvention of its customer loyalty program. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Walgreens is now offering the fastest <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">same-day</FONT> retail <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pick-up</FONT> in the U.S., with orders available in as little as 30 minutes. More than 1.7&nbsp;million <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pick-up</FONT> orders have been completed since launch in November.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Walgreens announced an acceleration of its investment in VillageMD and boosted the rollout of Village Medical at
Walgreens full-service primary care clinics. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Boots.com significantly expanded capacity and sales doubled from the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, outperforming the market. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Business Divisions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Retail Pharmacy USA: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail Pharmacy USA had first
quarter sales of $27.2&nbsp;billion, an increase of 3.9&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including the impact of previously announced store optimization programs. Sales in comparable stores increased
3.7&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter reflecting a 5.0&nbsp;percent increase in comparable pharmacy sales and a 0.4&nbsp;percent growth in comparable retail sales. The estimated adverse <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> impact on comparable sales included lower foot traffic in stores, weak retail cough, cold and flu sales, lower seasonal flu scripts and reduced <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">new-to-therapy</FONT></FONT> scripts. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In comparable stores, prescriptions filled in the first quarter increased
2.7&nbsp;percent from a year earlier, including an estimated negative impact of 210 basis points from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19.</FONT> Total prescriptions filled in the quarter increased 1.1&nbsp;percent, compared with the same
quarter a year earlier. The number of prescriptions filled was 297.3&nbsp;million, including immunizations, adjusted to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalents. Pharmacy sales, which accounted for 76.8&nbsp;percent of the
division&#146;s sales in the quarter, increased 5.9&nbsp;percent compared with the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Comparable pharmacy sales increased 5.0&nbsp;percent. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The division&#146;s retail prescription market share on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT>
adjusted basis in the first quarter decreased approximately 15 basis points over the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter to 20.7&nbsp;percent, as reported by IQVIA, an improvement over the decline in the fourth quarter and
entirely driven by store optimization programs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail sales decreased 2.2&nbsp;percent in the first quarter compared with the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, including the impact of the store optimization programs. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable retail sales grew 0.4&nbsp;percent
compared with the same quarter a year ago, held back by the significantly weaker cough, cold and flu season, which had an adverse impact of 150 basis points. Comparable retail sales, excluding tobacco and
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-cigarettes,</FONT> increased 1.9&nbsp;percent. Within comparable retail store sales, a 13.1&nbsp;percent decrease in beauty category sales and a 1.3&nbsp;percent decrease in personal care category sales were
partially offset by a 4.1&nbsp;percent increase in health and wellness category sales. Excluding the impact of the weaker cough, cold and flu season, sales in the health and wellness category increased by 11.6&nbsp;percent. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit decreased 1.3&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago and adjusted gross profit decreased 1.8&nbsp;percent, in both cases
primarily due to pharmacy reimbursement pressure, partly offset by pharmacy procurement savings and a higher retail gross margin. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First quarter SG&amp;A
decreased by 0.4&nbsp;percent, primarily due to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT> costs related to the acquisition of Rite Aid stores in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, and adjusted SG&amp;A
increased by 1.4&nbsp;percent, as cost savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program partly offset higher growth investments and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related costs of $83&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income in the first quarter decreased 6.6&nbsp;percent to $792&nbsp;million from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, due
to pharmacy reimbursement pressure and adverse impact from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</FONT> partly offset by savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-recurring</FONT>
acquisition-related costs related to Rite Aid stores in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. Adjusted operating income decreased 14.4&nbsp;percent, to $989&nbsp;million, due to pharmacy reimbursement pressure and adverse
impacts from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</FONT> partly offset by savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Retail
Pharmacy International: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Retail Pharmacy International had first quarter sales of $2.6&nbsp;billion, a decrease of 6.2&nbsp;percent from the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, including a favorable currency impact of 1.9&nbsp;percent. Sales decreased 8.2&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, mainly due to an 11.5&nbsp;percent decrease in Boots UK sales resulting
from <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> related impacts. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK comparable pharmacy sales increased 2.5&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, reflecting favorable timing of National Health System (NHS) reimbursement, which mitigated the impact of lower prescription volume and reduced demand for pharmacy services during the pandemic. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK comparable retail sales decreased 9.1&nbsp;percent compared to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> continued to impact footfall, particularly in major high street, train station and airport stores. The ongoing recovery in footfall trends in September and October was set back by the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-introduction</FONT> of stricter restrictions for the month of November. However, Boots.com continued to perform very strongly with sales up 106&nbsp;percent compared with the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, partially offsetting the reduced footfall. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Boots UK market share was lower in all categories
except beauty, as the pandemic continued to impact heavily on buying habits and consumers temporarily shifted purchasing to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-stop</FONT> grocery shopping. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Gross profit decreased 9.0&nbsp;percent compared with the same quarter a year ago, including a favorable currency impact of 2.3&nbsp;percent. Adjusted gross
profit decreased 11.5&nbsp;percent, on a constant currency basis, reflecting lower UK retail sales and higher fulfillment costs, partly offset by the favorable timing of NHS reimbursement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">SG&amp;A in the quarter decreased 8.4&nbsp;percent from the prior year quarter to $928&nbsp;million, including an adverse currency impact of 2.0&nbsp;percent.
On a constant currency basis, adjusted SG&amp;A decreased 12.5&nbsp;percent. The decreases in SG&amp;A and adjusted SG&amp;A both reflect short-term cost mitigation actions and cost savings from the Transformational Cost Management Program. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">3 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Operating income decreased 22.7&nbsp;percent to $34&nbsp;million, reflecting increased investment in the
Transformational Cost Management Program. Adjusted operating income was $84&nbsp;million, an increase of 6.4&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. On a constant currency basis, adjusted operating income
increased 0.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, as decisive cost management actions and strong Boots.com performance fully mitigated the impact of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19.</FONT> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Pharmaceutical Wholesale: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pharmaceutical Wholesale had
first quarter sales of $7.1&nbsp;billion, an increase of 18.6&nbsp;percent from the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter. On a constant currency basis, sales increased 16.3&nbsp;percent, including results of the company&#146;s
new joint venture in Germany, which were consolidated as of November. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The division had an operating loss of $1.3&nbsp;billion in the first quarter
entirely due to a loss of $1.4&nbsp;billion related to the company&#146;s equity method investment in AmerisourceBergen. This compared with operating income of $122&nbsp;million in the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> quarter, which
included $13&nbsp;million from the company&#146;s equity earnings in AmerisourceBergen. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Adjusted operating income increased 6.7&nbsp;percent to
$244&nbsp;million, up 7.4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis, reflecting strong sales growth and a higher contribution from AmerisourceBergen. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA will hold a conference call to
discuss the first quarter results beginning at 8:30 a.m. Eastern time today, Jan. 7, 2021. The conference call will be simulcast through the WBA investor relations website at: <U>http://investor.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. A replay of the
conference call will be archived on the website for 12 months after the call. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The replay also will be available from 11:30 a.m. Eastern time, Jan. 7
through Jan. 14, 2021, by calling +1 800 585 8367 within the U.S. and Canada, or +1 416 621 4642 outside the U.S. and Canada, using replay code 2692416. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>
including, but not limited to, those relating to the spread and impacts of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19,</FONT> any mutations thereof or future pandemic and the acceptance and
effectiveness of any therapies or vaccines related thereto, the impact of private and public third-party payers&#146; efforts to reduce prescription drug reimbursements, the risks associated with the withdrawal of the United Kingdom from the
European Union and the agreement related thereto, fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates, the timing and magnitude of the impact of branded to generic drug conversions and changes in generic drug prices, our ability to realize synergies and
achieve financial, tax and operating results in the amounts and at the times anticipated, the inherent risks, challenges and uncertainties associated with forecasting financial results of large, complex organizations in rapidly evolving industries,
particularly over longer time periods, and during periods with increased volatility and uncertainties, our supply, commercial and framework arrangements and transactions with AmerisourceBergen and their possible effects, the risks associated with
the company&#146;s equity method investment in AmerisourceBergen, circumstances that could give rise to the termination, cross-termination or modification of any of our contractual obligations, the amount of costs, fees, expenses and charges
incurred in connection with strategic transactions, whether the costs and charges associated with restructuring initiatives will exceed estimates, our ability to realize expected savings and benefits from cost-savings initiatives, restructuring
activities and acquisitions and joint ventures in the amounts and at the times anticipated, the timing and amount of any impairment or other charges, the timing and severity of cough, cold and flu season, risks relating to looting and vandalism in
regions in which we operate and the scope and magnitude of any property damage, inventory loss or other adverse impacts, risks related to pilot programs and new business initiatives and ventures generally, including the risks that anticipated
benefits may not be realized, changes in management&#146;s plans and assumptions, the risks associated with governance and control matters, the ability to retain key personnel, changes in economic and business conditions generally or in particular
markets in which we participate, changes in financial markets, credit ratings and interest rates, the risks relating to the terms, timing, and magnitude of any share repurchase activity, the risks associated with international business operations,
including international trade policies, tariffs (including tariff negotiations between the United States and China) and relations, the risks associated with cybersecurity or privacy breaches related to customer information, changes in vendor,
customer and payer relationships and terms, including changes in network participation and reimbursement terms and the associated impacts on volume and operating results, risks related to competition, including changes in market dynamics,
participants, product and service offerings, retail formats and competitive positioning, risks associated with new business areas and activities, risks associated with acquisitions, divestitures, joint ventures and strategic investments, including
those relating to the asset acquisition from Rite Aid and the sale of certain pharmaceutical wholesale operations to AmerisourceBergen, the risks associated with the integration of complex businesses, the impact of regulatory restrictions and
outcomes of legal and regulatory matters, and risks associated with changes in laws, including those related to tax law changes, regulations or interpretations thereof. These and other risks, assumptions and uncertainties are described in Item 1A
(Risk Factors) of our Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the fiscal year ended August&nbsp;31, 2020 and in other documents that we file or furnish with the Securities and Exchange Commission. Should one or more of
these risks or uncertainties materialize, or should underlying assumptions prove incorrect, actual results may vary materially from those indicated or anticipated by such forward-looking statements. All forward-looking statements we make or that are
made on our behalf are qualified by these cautionary statements. Accordingly, you are cautioned not to place undue reliance on these forward-looking statements, which speak only as of the date they are made. </I></P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Notes to Editors: </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Walgreens Boots Alliance </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Walgreens Boots Alliance
(Nasdaq: WBA) is a global leader in retail and wholesale pharmacy, touching millions of lives every day through dispensing and distributing medicines, its convenient retail locations, digital platforms and health and beauty products. The company has
more than 100 years of trusted health care heritage and innovation in community pharmacy and pharmaceutical wholesaling. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Including equity method
investments, WBA has a presence in more than 25 countries, employs more than 450,000 people and has more than 21,000 stores. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA&#146;s purpose is to
help people across the world lead healthier and happier lives. The company is proud of its contributions to healthy communities, a healthy planet, an inclusive workplace and a sustainable marketplace. WBA is a Participant of the United Nations
Global Compact and adheres to its principles-based approach to responsible business. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">WBA is included in FORTUNE&#146;s 2020 list of the World&#146;s Most
Admired Companies. This is the 27th consecutive year that WBA or its predecessor company, Walgreen Co., has been named to the list. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">More company
information is available at <U>www.walgreensbootsalliance.com</U>. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">*&copy; 2020, Fortune Media IP Limited.&nbsp;Used under license. </P>

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>WALGREENS BOOTS ALLIANCE, INC. AND SUBSIDIARIES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>SUPPLEMENTAL INFORMATION (UNAUDITED) </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>REGARDING <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-GAAP</FONT> FINANCIAL MEASURES </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">(in millions, except per share amounts) </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
following information provides reconciliations of the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures, as defined under SEC rules, presented in this press release to the most directly comparable financial measures
calculated and presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles in the United States (GAAP). The company has provided the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the press release, which are not
calculated or presented in accordance with GAAP, as supplemental information and in addition to the financial measures that are calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. Please refer to the notes to the &#147;Net Earnings and Diluted Net
Earnings (Loss) Per Share&#148; reconciliation table on page 13 for definitions of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures and related adjustments presented in this press release. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">These supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are presented because management has evaluated the company&#146;s
financial results both including and excluding the adjusted items or the effects of foreign currency translation, as applicable, and believes that the supplemental <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented provide
additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company&#146;s business from period to period and trends in the company&#146;s historical operating results. These supplemental
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures should not be considered superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented in the press
release. The company does not provide a reconciliation for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> estimates on a forward-looking basis (including the information under &#147;Company Outlook&#148; above) where it is unable to provide a
meaningful or accurate calculation or estimation of reconciling items and the information is not available without unreasonable effort. This is due to the inherent difficulty of forecasting the timing or amount of various items that have not yet
occurred, are out of the company&#146;s control and/or cannot be reasonably predicted, and that would impact diluted net earnings per share, the most directly comparable forward-looking GAAP financial measure. For the same reasons, the company is
unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information. Forward-looking <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures provided without the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures may vary materially
from the corresponding GAAP financial measures. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Constant currency </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company also presents certain information related to current period operating results in &#147;constant currency,&#148; which is a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. These amounts are calculated by translating current period results at the foreign currency exchange rates used in the comparable period in the prior year. The company presents such
constant currency financial information because it has significant operations outside of the United States reporting in currencies other than the U.S. dollar and this presentation provides a framework to assess how its business performed excluding
the impact of foreign currency exchange rate fluctuations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Comparable sales </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the company&#146;s Retail Pharmacy divisions, comparable sales are defined as sales from stores that have been open for at least 12 consecutive months
without closure for seven or more consecutive days, including due to looting or store damage, and without a major remodel or being subject to a natural disaster in the past 12 months as well as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT>
sales. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales include digitally initiated sales online or through mobile applications. Relocated stores are not included as comparable stores for the first 12 months after the relocation. Acquired
stores are not included as comparable sales for the first 12 months after acquisition or conversion, when applicable, whichever is later. Comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales, comparable retail sales, comparable number of prescriptions and
comparable number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent prescriptions refer to total sales, pharmacy sales, retail sales, number of prescriptions and number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT> equivalent
prescriptions, respectively. Comparable retail sales for previous periods have been restated to include <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sales. The method of calculating comparable sales varies across the retail industry. As a
result, the company&#146;s method of calculating comparable sales may not be the same as other retailers&#146; methods. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">10 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With respect to the Retail Pharmacy International division, comparable sales, comparable pharmacy sales and
comparable retail sales, are presented on a constant currency basis, which is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. Refer to the discussion above in &#147;Constant currency&#148; for further details on constant
currency calculations. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Key Performance Indicators </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The company considers certain metrics, including all comparable metrics, number of prescriptions, number of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">30-day</FONT>
equivalent prescriptions and number of locations at period end, to be key performance indicators because the company&#146;s management has evaluated its results of operations using these metrics and believes that these key performance indicators
presented provide additional perspective and insights when analyzing the core operating performance of the company from period to period and trends in its historical operating results. These key performance indicators should not be considered
superior to, as a substitute for or as an alternative to, and should be considered in conjunction with, the GAAP financial measures presented herein. These measures may not be comparable to similarly-titled performance indicators used by other
companies. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to equity earnings (loss) in AmerisourceBergen consist of the Company&#146;s proportionate share of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments reported by AmerisourceBergen consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. The Company recognized equity losses in AmerisourceBergen of
$1,373&nbsp;million during the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2020. These equity losses are primarily due to AmerisourceBergen recognition of $5.6&nbsp;billion, net of tax, charges related to its ongoing opioid litigation in its financial
statements for the three months period ended September&nbsp;30, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">2</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related amortization includes amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets and inventory
valuation adjustments. Amortization of acquisition-related intangible assets includes amortization of intangibles assets such as customer relationships, trade names, trademarks and contract intangibles. Intangible asset amortization excluded from
the related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measure represents the entire amount recorded within the Company&#146;s GAAP financial statements, the revenue generated by the associated intangible assets has not been excluded from the
related <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures. Amortization expense, unlike the related revenue, is not affected by operations of any particular period unless an intangible asset becomes impaired or the estimated useful life of
an intangible asset is revised. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. Business combination accounting principles require us to measure acquired inventory at fair value. The fair value of the
inventory reflects cost of acquired inventory and a portion of the expected profit margin. The acquisition-related inventory valuation adjustments excludes the expected profit margin component from cost of sales recorded under the business
combination accounting principles. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">3</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Transformational Cost Management Program and Store Optimization Program charges are costs associated with a
formal restructuring plan. These charges are primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs do not reflect current operating performance and are impacted by the timing of restructuring activity.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">4</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">The Company&#146;s Retail Pharmacy USA segment inventory is accounted for using the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">last-in-first-out</FONT></FONT></FONT> (&#147;LIFO&#148;) method. This adjustment represents the impact on cost of sales as if Retail Pharmacy USA segment
inventory is accounted for using <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in</FONT> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-out</FONT> (&#147;FIFO&#148;) method. The LIFO provision is affected by changes in inventory quantities, product mix, and
manufacturer pricing practices, which may be impacted by market and other external influences. Therefore, the Company cannot control the amounts recognized or timing of these items. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">5</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Acquisition-related costs are transaction and integration costs associated with certain merger and acquisition
related activities. These costs include all charges incurred on certain mergers and acquisition related activities, for example, including costs related to integration efforts for successful merger and acquisition activities. These charges are
primarily recorded within selling, general and administrative expenses. These costs are significantly impacted by the timing and complexity of the underlying merger and acquisition related activities and do not reflect the Company&#146;s current
operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">6</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Gain or loss on certain derivative instruments used as economic hedges of the Company&#146;s net investments in
foreign subsidiaries. These charges are recorded within other income (expense). We do not believe this volatility related to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mark-to-market</FONT></FONT> adjustment on the underlying
derivative instruments reflects the Company&#146;s operational performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">7</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Includes significant gain on sale of equity method investment and related adjustments. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">8</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to income tax provision include adjustments to the GAAP basis tax provision commensurate with <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments and certain discrete tax items including U.S. tax law changes, a UK tax rate change and equity method <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> tax. These charges are recorded within
income tax provision (benefit). </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">9</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Adjustments to post tax equity earnings from other equity method investments consist of the proportionate share
of certain equity method investees&#146; <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> items or unusual or infrequent items consistent with the Company&#146;s <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> adjustments. These charges are
recorded within post tax earnings (loss) from other equity method investments. Although the Company may have shareholder rights and board representation commensurate with its ownership interests in these equity method investees, adjustments relating
to equity method investments are not intended to imply that the Company has direct control over their operations and resulting revenue and expenses. Moreover, these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures have limitations
in that they do not reflect all revenue and expenses of these equity method investees. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">10</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Due to the anti-dilutive effect resulting from the reported net loss, the impact of potentially dilutive
securities on the per share amounts has been omitted from the quarterly calculation of weighted-average common shares outstanding for diluted earnings per share for the three months ended November&nbsp;30, 2020. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">1</SUP>&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Free cash flow is defined as net cash provided by operating activities in a period less additions to property,
plant and equipment (capital expenditures) made in that period.&nbsp;This measure does not represent residual cash flows available for discretionary expenditures as the measure does not deduct the payments required for debt service and other
contractual obligations or payments for future business acquisitions. Therefore, we believe it is important to view free cash flow as a measure that provides supplemental information to our entire statements of cash flows. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
